/**\n     * Fonction cachant les champs de l'adresse\n     */\n    function hideAddressInputs() {\n        jQuery('*[data-divid=\"street2\"]').hide();\n jQuery('*[data-divid=\"city\"]').show();\n            jQuery('*[data-divid=\"country\"]').show();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Fonction mettant à jour l'indicateur de fiabilité lorsqu'une        jQuery(document).ready(function () {\n            prepareQASValidation();\n        });\n\n        /**\n         * Fonctionn qui active la verification QAS\n         * @returns {undefined}\n         */\n        function prepareQASValidation()\n        {\n            var qassubmit = jQuery('*[data-qas=\"submit\"]');\n\n            qassubmit.each(function () {\n                var        * @returns {undefined}\n         */\n        function explicitLaunchQASValidation(form, callbackaction)\n        {\n            showWaitPanel();\n            prepareRequestQAS(form, inputToCorrect = jQuery(idEmailToCorrect);\n                inputToCorrect.val(jQuery(this).val());\n            }\n        });\n\n        hideErrorPanel();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Lance la * @returns {Boolean} false\n     */\n    function launchValidationQAS(btn, event, callbackAction) {\n\n        var qasform = jQuery(btn).closest(\"form\");\n\n        // Validate the form\n        if (qasform.valid()) {\n            showWaitPanel();\n\n            // checked data user input\n            prepareRequestQAS(qasform, callbackAction);\n\n            // block the post form\n            if( null !==  event ){\n                event.preventDefault();\n                event.stopPropagation();\n            }\n            \n            return false;\n        } else {\n            // block the post form\n            if( null !==  event ) {\n                event.preventDefault();\n                event.stopPropagation();\n            }\n            \n            return false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validation via QAS (Call Ajax)\n     * @param  {[object json]} datatovalidate [description]\n     * @param  {[formulaire]} form [description]\n     * @param  {[function]} callbackAction Obligation de passer ce param pour relancer les onclick inline catché précédemment\n     * @return {[type]}       [description]\n     */\n    function === false) {\n                    showErrorPanel(result);\n                } else {\n                    if (typeof callbackAction != 'undefined' && callbackAction != null) {\n                        callbackAction();\n                    }\n\n                    var btn = form.find('*[data-qas=\"submit\"]');\n                    btn.unbind('click').click();\n                    btn.bind('click', function () {\n                        launchValidationQAS(btn, null, callbackAction);\n                    });\n                    //form.submit();\n                }\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Vérification des données du formulaire renseigné\n     * @param  {[type]} form [description]\n     * @return {[type]} result_email [description]\n     */\n    function prepareRequestQAS(form, callbackAction) {\n        /**\n         * Récupérer les champs emails\n         */\n        var email_fields = form.find('*[data-qas=\"email\"]');\n        var aDataEmails = {};\n\n        jQuery.each(email_fields, function (key, value) {\n            if (jQuery(this).is(\":visible\")) {\n                var id = jQuery(this).attr('id');\n                var oEmail = {\n                    'email': jQuery(this).val()\n                };\n                aDataEmails[id] = oEmail;\n            }\n        });\n\n        /**\n         * Récupérer les champs téléphones\n         */\n        var phone_fields = form.find('*[data-qas=\"landline\"],*[data-qas=\"mobile\"]');\n        var aDataPhones = {};\n\n        jQuery.each(phone_fields, function (key, value) {\n            if (jQuery(this).is(\":visible\")) {\n                var id = jQuery(this).attr('id');\n                var oPhone = {\n                    'number': jQuery(this).val(),\n                    'countrycode': form.find('*[data-qas=\"country\"] option:selected').val(),\n                    'type': jQuery(this).data('qas')\n                };\n\n                if (jQuery(this).val() != '') {\n                    aDataPhones[id] = oPhone;\n                }\n            }\n        });\n\n        /**\n         * Récupérer les champs adresses\n         */\n        var aDataAddresses = {};\n        var oAddress = {\n            'firstname': form.find('*[data-qas=\"firstname\"]').val(),\n            'lastname': form.find('*[data-qas=\"lastname\"]').val(),\n            'street1': form.find('*[data-qas=\"street1\"]').val(),\n            'street2': form.find('*[data-qas=\"street2\"]').val(),\n            'postcode': form.find('*[data-qas=\"postcode\"]').val(),\n            'city': form.find('*[data-qas=\"city\"]').val(),\n            'countrycode': form.find('*[data-qas=\"country\"] option:selected').val(),\n            'reliability': form.find('*[data-qas=\"reliability\"]').val()\n        };\n\n        if (typeof oAddress.street1 != 'undefined' && oAddress.street1 != '') {\n            aDataAddresses['address_id1'] = oAddress;\n        }\n\n        // Fusionner toutes les datas à envoyer au ProcessController\n        var dataToInsert = {\"emails\": aDataEmails, \"phones\": aDataPhones, \"addresses\": aDataAddresses};\n\n        sendRequestQAS(JSON.stringify(dataToInsert), form, callbackAction); // -> call Ajax\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Détecter si champ non valide dans la réponse QAS\n     * @param  {[object]}  result [Json retourné par QAS]\n     * @return {Boolean}        [true si erreur, false si pas d'erreur]\n     */\n    function isDataValidatedByQAS(result) {\n        if (result.isValid == true) {\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Show waiting popin\n     * @return void\n     */\n    function showWaitPanel() {\n        Element.show('popup_wait_qas');\n        jQuery('body').addClass('hidemain');\n        scrollToPopin('#popup_wait_qas');\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Hide waiting popin\n     * @return void\n     */\n    function hideWaitPanel() {\n        Element.hide('popup_wait_qas');\n        jQuery('body').removeClass('hidemain');\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Show errors popin\n     * @param  {[object]} result JSON QAS\n     * @return void\n     */\n    function showErrorPanel(result) {\n        makeContentPanel(result);\n        Element.show('popup_err_qas');\n        jQuery('body').addClass('hidemain');\n        scrollToPopin('#popup_err_qas');\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Hide errors popin\n     * @return void\n     */\n    function hideErrorPanel() {\n        Element.hide('popup_err_qas');\n        jQuery('body').removeClass('hidemain');\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Gérer l'affichage des erreurs QAS\n     * @param  {[object]} result JSON QAS\n     * @return void\n     */\n    function makeContentPanel(result) {\n        var html_content = '<form id=\"other-emails\">';\n        html_content += \"<div id='logerr_message'><h2>Certains champs n'ont pas pû être validés :</h2></div>\";\n\n        if (typeof result.phones != 'undefined') {\n            html_content += displayPhoneResponse(result.phones);\n        }\n\n        if (typeof result.emails != 'undefined') {\n            html_content += displayEmailResponse(result.emails);\n        }\n\n        if (typeof result.addresses != 'undefined') {\n            html_content += displayAddressesResponse(result.addresses);\n        }\n\n        html_content += '</form>';\n\n        jQuery('#err_qas_message').html(html_content);\n        \n        jQuery('.email_correction').change(function () {\n            jQuery('#buttonValidateEmailCorrection').prop('disabled', false);\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Display Phones Error QAS Response\n     * @param  {[object]} result - JSON QAS\n     * @return {[string]} Content html\n     */\n    function displayPhoneResponse(phones) {\n        var phone_html_content = \"\";\n\n        jQuery.each(phones, function (key, value) {\n            if (typeof value.isValid != 'undefined' && value.isValid != true) {\n\n                // Get phone type (mobile/landline)\n                key_id = jq(key);\n                phone_type = jQuery(key_id).data('qas');\n\n                phone_html_content += \"<dl class='dl-error-message'>\";\n                if (phone_type == 'mobile') {\n                    phone_html_content += \"<dt>Téléphone portable</dt>\";\n                } else {\n \"</dl>\";\n            }\n        });\n\n        return phone_html_content;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Display Mail Error QAS Response\n     * @param  {[object]} result - JSON QAS\n     * @return {[string]} Content html\n     */\n    function displayEmailResponse(emails) {\n        var email_html_content = \"\";\n\n        jQuery.each(emails, function (key, value) {\n email_html_content += \"<div><h2>Cependant nous avons trouvé des adresses se rapprochant de l'email : <span class='pink'>\\\"\" + emailToCorrect + \"\\\"</span>.</h2></div><br/>\";\n                 jQuery.each(value.corrections, function (key2, value2) {\n                        email_html_content += '<div class=\"other-emails-email\"><input type=\"radio\" name=\"' + key +
